<div id="review_2942584384" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2942584384" />
    <a title="Ash" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/57274851-ash"><img alt="Ash" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1603895397p2/57274851.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2942584384?book_show_action=true">Oct 05, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ash" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ash" href="/user/show/57274851-ash">Ash</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/42364684-practical-magic">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">fans of magical realism and romance</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57274851-ash?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57274851-ash?shelf=read-2019">read-2019</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57274851-ash?shelf=2-stars">2-stars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2942584384" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6812698391619529829">The tone of this book could not be more perfectly suited to its subject matter. Alice Hoffman’s writing style is reminiscent of a fairy tale. From the very first page, I was hooked, not because the story was action-packed or because it kept me on the edge of my seat wondering what would happen next, but because it was enchanting and immersive. I wanted to sink into this fantasy world and never leave. For the first thirty pages, as Hoffman writes about Sally and Gillian’s childhood, my hopes were</span>
  <span id="freeText6812698391619529829" style="display:none">The tone of this book could not be more perfectly suited to its subject matter. Alice Hoffman’s writing style is reminiscent of a fairy tale. From the very first page, I was hooked, not because the story was action-packed or because it kept me on the edge of my seat wondering what would happen next, but because it was enchanting and immersive. I wanted to sink into this fantasy world and never leave. For the first thirty pages, as Hoffman writes about Sally and Gillian’s childhood, my hopes were high that this would be one of the most magical books I’ve ever read.<br /><br />Unfortunately, as Sally and Gillian grew older and left their aunts’ home in Massachusetts to make their own way in the world, the sense of magic faded. It was still there, never disappearing fully from the narrative, but it took a backseat to the book's other pervading theme: love. I wouldn’t classify <i>Practical Magic</i> as a romance novel because the focus is on the concept of love rather than on any particular couple. I’m fully on board with the concept of a book that explores the intersection of love and magic; rather, it was Hoffman’s execution of the concept that didn't quite do it for me.<br /><br />Hoffman’s frequent use of hyperbolic language works when she’s describing magical phenomena, but when she’s describing attraction and romance, it’s too much. Each of the four main characters – Sally, Gillian, Antonia, and Kylie – are, at various points in the book, the most beautiful women you could possibly imagine. Men lose their minds around them and other women are driven mad with jealousy. When two characters enter a romantic relationship, they fall head over heels almost instantaneously. They aren’t just in love; they’re obsessed. They aren’t just attracted to each other; they’re so overcome with desire they can barely function in their daily lives.<br /><br />Additionally, the way Hoffman switched back and forth between past and present tense was confusing. I could never tell when, exactly, the “present” was. I think the writing would have flowed better if it was written entirely in past tense. I enjoyed <i>Practical Magic</i> to an extent, but I was disappointed that it didn’t live up to my expectations. It had the potential to be a truly magical read but instead left me wanting. I’m still going to read <i>The Rules of Magic</i> because I’ve already borrowed my mom's copy. Maybe I’ll be able to enjoy it more now that I know what to expect.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6812698391619529829" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1732587243" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1732587243" />
    <a title="Linda Hart" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2455252-linda-hart"><img alt="Linda Hart" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1549256566p2/2455252.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1732587243?book_show_action=true">Apr 27, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Linda Hart" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Linda Hart" href="/user/show/2455252-linda-hart">Linda Hart</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1732587243" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11186458788154301487">This is a beautifully written, quirky adult fairytale. If you enjoy reading magical realism you will love this. The characters are likable and well drawn, the descriptive prose is lovely, and the story is just plain fun.</span>

          </span>

I've read it twice now, and in a year or so will be ready for a re-read. The movie is good, too, but I love the book best, An Utterly Delightful novel about the magic of life.<br/><br/>From the Publisher<br/>Practical Magic is <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5693.Selected_Stories' title='Selected Stories by Anton Chekhov' rel='nofollow noopener'>a tale of two sisters</a>, Gillian and Sally Owens, brought up by their two elderly guardian aunts in a world of spells and exotica from which they eventually escape - one by running away, the other by marryi</span>
  <span id="freeText2875226813144946158" style="display:none">2007 reviewI just love this book, really. It makes me smile just to think about it. I've read it twice now, and in a year or so will be ready for a re-read. The movie is good, too, but I love the book best, An Utterly Delightful novel about the magic of life.<br /><br />From the Publisher<br />Practical Magic is <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5693.Selected_Stories" title="Selected Stories by Anton Chekhov" rel="nofollow noopener">a tale of two sisters</a>, Gillian and Sally Owens, brought up by their two elderly guardian aunts in a world of spells and exotica from which they eventually escape - one by running away, the other by marrying - but which never escapes from them. Many years go by before strange circumstances thrust them together again, and again they are in a world that blends the mundane and the mysterious, the familiar and the fantastic, the normal and the numinous. Three generations of Owens women are then united in an experience of unexpected insight and revelation, teaching all of them that the perceptions provided by what is called the magical are rare and wonderful endowments.<br /><br />2017 review: Fun to listen to on audio after reading the recently published <i>The Rules of Magic</i> which is a prequel. Husband wanted to read it so we listened to the book on audible. Didn't hold up as well as I'd have liked, and while we did enjoy it, I have to agree with Javaczuk that Hoffman's style of description is a little like the "Most interesting man in the world" commercials.</span>

<div id="review_2186607975" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2186607975" />
    <a title="Fred Shaw" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44212467-fred-shaw"><img alt="Fred Shaw" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1545362118p2/44212467.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2186607975?book_show_action=true">Nov 19, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Fred Shaw" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Fred Shaw" href="/user/show/44212467-fred-shaw">Fred Shaw</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audiobook 9780743545655" href="/book/show/7427531-practical-magic">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2186607975" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4906505008230490259">Practical Magic, by Alice Hoffman, narrated by Christina Moore, Simon and Schuster Audio Books<br/><br/>Imagine for a moment, a steaming cauldron, and some ancient woman in a black coat pouring in a huge heaping of Alice Hoffman and stirring in a little Stephen King. Do you think one might get “Practical Magic” as the result? What a great story about a family of 2 aunts who live in an ancient family home in Massachusetts, with windows no one can see in or see out, 2 adopted nieces, one when grown has 2 li</span>
  <span id="freeText4906505008230490259" style="display:none">Practical Magic, by Alice Hoffman, narrated by Christina Moore, Simon and Schuster Audio Books<br /><br />Imagine for a moment, a steaming cauldron, and some ancient woman in a black coat pouring in a huge heaping of Alice Hoffman and stirring in a little Stephen King. Do you think one might get “Practical Magic” as the result? What a great story about a family of 2 aunts who live in an ancient family home in Massachusetts, with windows no one can see in or see out, 2 adopted nieces, one when grown has 2 little girls. This is no ordinary family by any means. Beautiful women in stature that can attract men like bees to honey. There is an aura about them as well that makes the neighbors bring in their children and hide their husbands.<br /><br />This is such a popular story that so many have read and/or seen the movie that I cannot add another idea. If I told any more of the story, I would bound to give away some snippet spoiler and ruin the book for an unsuspecting reader. It’s a little scary but mostly hilarious with laugh out loud moments. I highly recommend this to men and women and young adults. There is a little rough language that I might warn of, but I think added terrific color. If you are interested in an audio book version, I recommend this one by Simon and Schuster. Christina Moore tells the story so well.<br /><br />ENJOY!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="4906505008230490259" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3298951040" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3298951040" />
    <a title="Susanne  Strong" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4514828-susanne-strong"><img alt="Susanne  Strong" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1583087410p2/4514828.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3298951040?book_show_action=true">May 10, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Susanne  Strong" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Susanne  Strong" href="/user/show/4514828-susanne-strong">Susanne  Strong</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4514828-susanne-strong?shelf=re-read">re-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4514828-susanne-strong?shelf=library-book">library-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4514828-susanne-strong?shelf=audiobooks">audiobooks</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3298951040" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9723512490656484390">3 Stars<br/><br/>After having read “Magic Lessons” by Alice Hoffman, which is the prequel to “Practical Magic” and “The Rules of Magic” - I decided to go back and re-read “Practical Magic” as it had been about 20 years since I’d read it and while my memory is good, it’s not that good. <br/><br/>What did I discover? Well, I discovered that I absolutely loved “The Rules of Magic” and “Magic Lessons” but that “Practical Magic” was a lot less magical this time around. That in fact, very little happened to give me a twi</span>
  <span id="freeText9723512490656484390" style="display:none">3 Stars<br /><br />After having read “Magic Lessons” by Alice Hoffman, which is the prequel to “Practical Magic” and “The Rules of Magic” - I decided to go back and re-read “Practical Magic” as it had been about 20 years since I’d read it and while my memory is good, it’s not that good. <br /><br />What did I discover? Well, I discovered that I absolutely loved “The Rules of Magic” and “Magic Lessons” but that “Practical Magic” was a lot less magical this time around. That in fact, very little happened to give me a twinkle in my eye or a jig in my step. Though I loved the characters of Sally and Gillian Owens, as well as Sally’s children - they unfortunately, were not enough to save this story. If I needed to conjure magic, I’d have to hope against hope that either Maria Owens (from Magic Lessons), Franny, Jet or Vincent (from The Rules of Magic) would come and save me because neither Sally or Gillian could do the trick since they ran from magic their entire lives. <br /><br />Perhaps my tastes have changed as I recall loving this when I was younger. I am grateful however, that Ms. Hoffman wrote the prequels as she has raised the bar and I hope she continues to do so.<br /><br />Thank you to my local library for loaning me the audiobook of this novel. <br /><br />Published on Goodreads on 5.10.20.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9723512490656484390" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('YhigLlu6f23kD1AzGTWd4k6wQTVrLdQNl2eQpimRBv9JzBVUZLg7Wsj4GdDXLyyRVpF2MR8Ue0nD5fRz4qWNkw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('/r9OwS/sNL8LCUg6CD6N3Jb4JdotPiyfoYEAJ8bnksnVa/u7EO5wiCf+AdnGJDyvjtkS3lkHg9v1A2TyDdMZpQ==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer15189890052960924473">Alice Hoffman is the author of more than thirty works of fiction, including The World That We Knew, The Rules of Magic, The Marriage of Opposites, Practical Magic, The Red Garden, the Oprah’s Book Club selection Here on Earth, The Museum of Extraordinary Things, and The Dovekeepers. Her most recent novel is The World That We Knew. She lives near Boston.</span>

</div>
